This is ideal for drying protocols with very tight temperature requirements. The 4.3-inch touchscreen controller provides fast, accurate, and uniform heat displacement. Users can preset 8 periods and 8 steps for a total of 64 programs. Temperature, time and fan speed can be set and programmed at the same time. The doors are engineered with airtight sealing and inner chambers are designed with corrosion resistant stainless steel. Safety alarms are installed for – overtemperature, over current protection, and temperature deviation. These ovens provide excellent temperature stability and reproducibility for all your desired application needs ensuring maximum efficiency, safety, and ease of use.">

            <section class="container" id="product_full_spec">
                
                
                    <h3 class="product_info_heading_para_class">
                      PRODUCT INFO
                    </h3>
            <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-md-10">
                        <div class="totus_product_specification_div">
                            
                                <div class="sort_description_div_main">
                                    <p class="sort_description_p">The BOF Forced-air Convection Drying Oven series distributes heat evenly inside the chamber with an integrated fan. This is ideal for drying protocols with very tight temperature requirements. The 4.3-inch touchscreen controller provides fast, accurate, and uniform heat displacement. Users can preset 8 periods and 8 steps for a total of 64 programs. Temperature, time and fan speed can be set and programmed at the same time. The doors are engineered with airtight sealing and inner chambers are designed with corrosion resistant stainless steel. Safety alarms are installed for – overtemperature, over current protection, and temperature deviation. These ovens provide excellent temperature stability and reproducibility for all your desired application needs ensuring maximum efficiency, safety, and ease of use.</p>
                                </div>

                <div class="tab-pane fade" id="faqs">
                    <div id="1808">
                        <div>
                            <div class="accordion faqlist" id="faqlist">
                                <div class="card">
                                    <div class="card-header" id="heading1">
                                        <h2 class="mb-0">
                                            <button class="btns btn-link btn-block text-left" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapseOne" data-target="#collapse1">My oven's display has Chinese characters on it. What do I do?</button>
                                        </h2>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="collapse" data-parent="#faqlist" id="collapse1">
                                        <div class="card-body"><p>The Chinese characters on the display can happen for a couple of reasons. One is someone was touching the screen during power up. Please download and follow the <a href="/web/image/40802/DOC_BEING-ChineseDisplayInstructions_V2_20230606.pdf" target="_blank">troubleshooting instructions</a>.<br></p></div>
                                    </div>
                                </div><div class="card">
                                    <div class="card-header" id="heading6">
                                        <h2 class="mb-0">
                                            <button class="btns btn-link btn-block text-left" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapseOne" data-target="#collapse6">Does the controller have the capability to adjust the ramp rate?</button>
                                        </h2>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="collapse" data-parent="#faqlist" id="collapse6">
                                        <div class="card-body"><p>No. However, the speed at which the oven reaches your desired setpoint can be controlled via the fan speed (BOF Series only), the adjustable exhaust port, and a multi-step program.</p><p><b>Fan speed (BOF Models only): </b>The fan speed controls three elements of the oven: the volume of air being circulated in the chamber, the amount of ambient air being drawn into the chamber and over the heating element, and the baking time.</p><p>Operating the oven’s fan on high (100%) will speed up the reaching of the setpoint while running it on low (50%) will cause the oven to reach the setpoint more slowly. This is due to the volume of air circulating through the chamber and across the heater.</p><p>A high (100%) fan speed draws more ambient air into the chamber, while a low (50%) fan speed draws in less ambient air.</p><p>The fan speed also impacts the volume of air (humidity) leaving the oven through the adjustable exhaust port.</p><p><b>Adjustable exhaust port:&nbsp;</b> Closing the vent will retain the humidity in the oven, causing a slower heat rise. It also reduces the number of heat exchanges by not allowing ambient air to be drawn into the oven’s chamber and over the heating element. </p><p>Opening the vent will allow the humidity to dissipate, speeding up the heating process, allowing more ambient air to be drawn into the chamber, and speeding up baking.</p><p><b> Multi-step programs:</b> You can control how quickly you reach the desired setpoint by stepping from one temperature to another, holding for a period for the temperature to stabilize, and repeating this process until you reach the final (desired) setpoint. </p><p>No matter what fan speed you utilize, how open or closed the adjustable exhaust vent is, or whether you use a fixed-value or multi-step program, you will notice two things.</p><ol><li><p>The oven starts heating rapidly, and as it closes in on the setpoint, the heating slows down so as not to overshoot the setpoint.</p></li><li><p>The larger the difference between chamber temperature and the setpoint, the faster the rise. The smaller the differential between chamber temperature and setpoint, the longer it takes to reach the setpoint. This is especially important to understand when using multistep programs.</p></li></ol><p>For example, if the oven chamber is at ambient (20-25<sup>O</sup>C) and the setpoint is 200<sup>O</sup>C, the oven will ramp up faster than if, at the end of a step, the chamber temperature is at 150<sup>O</sup>C and the setpoint is 200<sup>O</sup>C.&nbsp;</p><p>Other factors impacting the setpoint reach and baking times include the number/volume of specimens, samples, or parts, their mass, the type(s) of materials in the specimens, samples, or parts, and their density inside the chamber. Density means they are packed close together or separated by some distance.&nbsp;</p><p>To optimize air circulation, we supply wire racks and recommend distributing specimens, samples, or parts evenly throughout the chamber.</p><div><br></div></div>
                                    </div>
                                </div><div class="card">
                                    <div class="card-header" id="heading7">
                                        <h2 class="mb-0">
                                            <button class="btns btn-link btn-block text-left" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapseOne" data-target="#collapse7">Are there any software updates for the controller?</button>
                                        </h2>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="collapse" data-parent="#faqlist" id="collapse7">
                                        <div class="card-body"><p>No, and yes. On units with manufacturing (production) dates after January 1, 2023, the firmware can be updated by inserting a USB drive into the data collection port. Units built before January 1, 2023, <b>CANNOT </b>have the controller’s firmware updated.<br></p></div>
                                    </div>
                                </div><div class="card">
                                    <div class="card-header" id="heading88">
                                        <h2 class="mb-0">
                                            <button class="btns btn-link btn-block text-left" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapseOne" data-target="#collapse88">When using multi-step programs, can you automatically jump from one program to another?</button>
                                        </h2>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="collapse" data-parent="#faqlist" id="collapse88">
                                        <div class="card-body"><p>No.</p></div>
                                    </div>
                                </div><div class="card">
                                    <div class="card-header" id="heading172">
                                        <h2 class="mb-0">
                                            <button class="btns btn-link btn-block text-left" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapseOne" data-target="#collapse172">Does modifying my BEING instrument void the warranty?</button>
                                        </h2>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="collapse" data-parent="#faqlist" id="collapse172">
                                        <div class="card-body"><p>Yes.</p></div>
                                    </div>
                                </div><div class="card">
                                    <div class="card-header" id="heading295">
                                        <h2 class="mb-0">
                                            <button class="btns btn-link btn-block text-left" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapseOne" data-target="#collapse295">Where do I find my unit's model, serial numbers, and manufacturing (production) date?</button>
                                        </h2>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="collapse" data-parent="#faqlist" id="collapse295">

                                    </div>
                                </div><div class="card">
                                    <div class="card-header" id="heading399">
                                        <h2 class="mb-0">
                                            <button class="btns btn-link btn-block text-left" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapseOne" data-target="#collapse399">Will the over-setpoint (&gt;SV+AL) and under-setpoint (&lt;SV-AL) alarms automatically turn off when the instruments' temperature returns to the appropriate temperature?</button>
                                        </h2>
                                    </div>

                                </div><div class="card">
